The batch will be fully closed (ie. the record batch headers will be written\\n422:      *  and memory records built) in one of the following cases (whichever comes first): right before send,\\n423:      *  if it is expired, or when the producer is closed.\\n424:      */\\n425:     private RecordAppendResult tryAppend(long timestamp, byte[] key, byte[] value, Header[] headers,\\n426: Hence we do not do the delivery timeout check here.\\n495:      */\\n496:     public void reenqueue(ProducerBatch batch, long now) {\\n497:         batch.reenqueued(now);\\n498:         Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getOrCreateDeque(batch.topicPartition);\\n499:         synchronized (deque) {\\n500:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n501:                 insertInSequenceOrder(deque, batch);\\n502:             else\\n503:                 deque.addFirst(batch);\\n504:         }\\n505:     }\\n506: \\n507:     /**\\n508:      * Split the big batch that has been rejected and reenqueue the split batches in to the accumulator.\\n509:      * @return the number of split batches.\\n510:      */\\n511:     public int splitAndReenqueue(ProducerBatch bigBatch) {\\n512:         // Reset the estimated compression ratio to the initial value or the big batch compression ratio, whichever\\n513:         // is bigger. There are several different ways to do the reset. We chose the most conservative one to ensure\\n514:         // the split doesn't happen too often.\\n515:         CompressionRatioEstimator.setEstimation(bigBatch.topicPartition.topic(), compression.type(),\\n516:                                                 Math.max(1.0f, (float) bigBatch.compressionRatio()));\\n517:         Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = bigBatch.split(this.batchSize);\\n518:         int numSplitBatches = dq.size();\\n519:         Deque<ProducerBatch> partitionDequeue = getOrCreateDeque(bigBatch.topicPartition);\\n520:         while (!dq.isEmpty()) {\\n521:             ProducerBatch batch = dq.pollLast();\\n522:             incomplete.add(batch);\\n523:             // We treat the newly split batches as if they are not even tried.\\n524:             synchronized (partitionDequeue) {\\n525:                 if (transactionManager != null) {\\n526:                     // We should track the newly created batches since they already have assigned sequences.\\n527:                     transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\\n528:                     insertInSequenceOrder(partitionDequeue, batch);\\n529:                 } else {\\n530:                     partitionDequeue.addFirst(batch);\\n531:                 }\\n532:             }\\n533:         }\\n534:         return numSplitBatches;\\n535:     }\\n536: \\n537:     // We will have to do extra work to ensure the queue is in order when requests are being retried and there are\\n538:     // multiple requests in flight to that partition. If the first in flight request fails to append, then all the\\n539:     // subsequent in flight requests will also fail because the sequence numbers will not be accepted.\\n540:     //\\n541:     // Further, once batches are being retried, we are reduced to a single in flight request for that partition. So when\\n542:     // the subsequent batches come back in sequence order, they will have to be placed further back in the queue.\\n543:     //\\n544:     // Note that this assumes that all the batches in the queue which have an assigned sequence also have the current\\n545:     // producer id. We will not attempt to reorder messages if the producer id has changed, we will throw an\\n546:     // IllegalStateException instead.\\n547:     private void insertInSequenceOrder(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, ProducerBatch batch) {\\n548:         // When we are re-enqueueing and have enabled idempotence, the re-enqueued batch must always have a sequence.\\n549:         if (batch.baseSequence() == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\\n550:             throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Trying to re-enqueue a batch which doesn't have a sequence even \\\" +\\n551:                 \\\"though idempotency is enabled.\\\");\\n552: \\n553:         if (!transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(batch.topicPartition))\\n554:             throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"We are re-enqueueing a batch which is not tracked as part of the in flight \\\" +\\n555:                 \\\"requests. batch.topicPartition: \\\" + batch.topicPartition + \\\"; It was placed in the queue at \\\" +\\n572:                 \\\"position {}\\\", batch.baseSequence(), batch.topicPartition, orderedBatches.size());\\n573:             // Either we have reached a point where there are batches without a sequence (ie. never been drained\\n574:             // and are hence in order by default), or the batch at the front of the queue has a sequence greater\\n575:             // than the incoming batch. This is the right place to add the incoming batch.\\n576:             deque.addFirst(batch);\\n577: \\n578:             // Now we have to re insert the previously queued batches in the right order.\\n579:             for (int i = orderedBatches.size() - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\\n580:                 deque.addFirst(orderedBatches.get(i));\\n581:             }\\n582: \\n583:             // At this point, the incoming batch has been queued in the correct place according to its sequence.\\n584:         } else {\\n585:             deque.addFirst(batch);\\n586:         }\\n587:     }\\n588: \\n589:     /**\\n590:      * Add the leader to the ready nodes if the batch is ready\\n591:      *\\n592:      * @param exhausted 'true' is the buffer pool is exhausted\\n593:      * @param part The partition\\n594:      * @param leader The leader for the partition\\n595:      * @param waitedTimeMs How long batch waited\\n596:      * @param backingOff Is backing off\\n597:      * @param backoffAttempts Number of attempts for calculating backoff delay\\n598:      * @param full Is batch full\\n599:      * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\\n600:      * @param readyNodes The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\\n601:      * @return The delay for next check\\n602:      */\\n603:     private long batchReady(boolean exhausted, TopicPartition part, Node leader,\\n604:                             long waitedTimeMs, boolean backingOff, int backoffAttempts,\\n605:                             boolean full, long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes) {\\n606:         if (!readyNodes.contains(leader) && !isMuted(part)) {\\n607:             long timeToWaitMs = backingOff ? retryBackoff.backoff(backoffAttempts > 0 ? backoffAttempts - 1 : 0) : lingerMs;\\n608:             boolean expired = waitedTimeMs >= timeToWaitMs;\\n609:             boolean transactionCompleting = transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isCompleting();\\n610:             boolean sendable = full\\n611:                     || expired\\n612:                     || exhausted\\n613:                     || closed\\n614:                     || flushInProgress()\\n615:                     || transactionCompleting;\\n616:             if (sendable && !backingOff) {\\n617:                 readyNodes.add(leader);\\n618:             } else {\\n619:                 long timeLeftMs = Math.max(timeToWaitMs - waitedTimeMs, 0);\\n620:                 // Note that this results in a conservative estimate since an un-sendable partition may have\\n621:                 // a leader that will later be found to have sendable data. <p>\\n747:      * A destination node is ready to send data if:\\n748:      * <ol>\\n749:      * <li>There is at least one partition that is not backing off its send\\n750:      * <li><b>and</b> those (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n795:             if (shouldBackoff) {\\n796:                 log.trace(\\n797:                     \\\"For {}, will backoff\\\", batch);\\n798:             } else {\\n799: first.baseSequence() != firstInFlightSequence;\\n843:         }\\n844:         return false;\\n845:     }\\n846: \\n847:     private List<ProducerBatch> drainBatchesForOneNode(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, Node node, int maxSize, long now) {\\n848:         int size = 0;\\n849:         List<PartitionInfo> parts = metadataSnapshot.cluster().partitionsForNode(node.id());\\n850: */\\n854:         int drainIndex = getDrainIndex(node.idString());\\n855:         int start = drainIndex = drainIndex % parts.size();\\n856:         do {\\n857:             PartitionInfo part = partitionInfo.partition();\n304:                 } else {\n305:                     partitionInfo = null;\n306:                     effectivePartition = partition;\n307:                 }\n308: \n309: in-progress batch\n313:                 Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = topicInfo.batches.computeIfAbsent(effectivePartition, k -> new ArrayDeque<>());\n314:                 synchronized (dq) {\n315:                     // After taking the lock, validate that the partition hasn't changed and retry.\n316:                     if (partitionChanged(topic, topicInfo, partitionInfo, dq, nowMs, cluster))\n317:                         continue;\n318: \n319:                     RecordAppendResult appendResult = tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, dq, nowMs);\n320:                     if (appendResult != null) {\n321:                         // If queue has incomplete batches we disable switch (see comments in updatePartitionInfo).\n322:                         boolean enableSwitch = allBatchesFull(dq);\n323:                         topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, appendResult.appendedBytes, cluster, enableSwitch);\n324:                         return appendResult;\n325:                     }\n326:                 }\n327: \n328:                 if (buffer == null) {\n329:                     int size = Math.max(this.batchSize, AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytesUpperBound(\n330:                             RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression.type(), key, value, headers));\n331:                     log.trace(\"Allocating a new {} byte message buffer for topic {} partition {} with remaining timeout {}ms\", size, topic, effectivePartition, maxTimeToBlock);\n332:                     // This call may block if we exhausted buffer space.\n333:                     buffer = free.allocate(size, maxTimeToBlock);\n334:                     // Update the current time in case the buffer allocation blocked above.\n335:                     // NOTE: getting time may be expensive, so calling it under a lock\n336:                     // should be avoided.\n337:                     nowMs = time.milliseconds();\n338:                 }\n339: \n340:                 synchronized (dq) {\n341:                     // After taking the lock, validate that the partition hasn't changed and retry.\n342:                     if (partitionChanged(topic, topicInfo, partitionInfo, dq, nowMs, cluster))\n343:                         continue;\n344: \n345:                     RecordAppendResult appendResult = appendNewBatch(topic, effectivePartition, dq, timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, buffer, nowMs);\n346:                     // Set buffer to null, so that deallocate doesn't return it back to free pool, since it's used in the batch.\n347:                     if (appendResult.newBatchCreated)\n348:                         buffer = null;\n349:                     // If queue has incomplete batches we disable switch (see comments in updatePartitionInfo).\n350:                     boolean enableSwitch = allBatchesFull(dq);\n351:                     topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, appendResult.appendedBytes, cluster, enableSwitch);\n352:                     return appendResult;\n353:                 }\n354:             }\n355:         } finally {\n356:             free.deallocate(buffer);\n357:             appendsInProgress.decrementAndGet();\n358:         }\n359:     }\n360: \n361:     /**\n362:      * Append a new batch to the queue\n363:      *\n364:      * @param topic The topic\n365:      * @param partition The partition (cannot be RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION)\n366:      * @param dq The queue\n367:      * @param timestamp The timestamp of the record\n368:      * @param key The key for the record\n369:      * @param value The value for the record\n370:      * @param headers the Headers for the record\n371:      * @param callbacks The callbacks to execute\n372:      * @param buffer The buffer for the new batch\n373:      * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n374:      */\n375:     private RecordAppendResult appendNewBatch(String topic,\n376:                                               int partition,\n377:                                               Deque<ProducerBatch> dq,\n378:                                               long timestamp,\n379:                                               byte[] key,\n380:                                               byte[] value,\n381:                                               Header[] headers,\n382:                                               AppendCallbacks callbacks,\n383:                                               ByteBuffer buffer,\n384:                                               long nowMs) {\n385:         assert partition != RecordMetadata.UNKNOWN_PARTITION;\n386: \n387:         RecordAppendResult appendResult = tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callbacks, dq, nowMs);\n388:         if (appendResult != null) {\n389:             // Somebody else found us a batch, return the one we waited for! Hopefully this doesn't happen often...\n390:             return appendResult;\n391:         }\n392: \n393:         MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder = recordsBuilder(buffer);\n394:         ProducerBatch batch = new ProducerBatch(new TopicPartition(topic, partition), recordsBuilder, nowMs);\n395:         FutureRecordMetadata future = Objects.requireNonNull(batch.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers,\n396:                 callbacks, nowMs));\n397: \n398:         dq.addLast(batch);\n399:         incomplete.add(batch);\n400: \n401:         return new RecordAppendResult(future, dq.size() > 1 || batch.isFull(), true, batch.estimatedSizeInBytes());\n402:     }\n403: \n404:     private MemoryRecordsBuilder recordsBuilder(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n405:         return MemoryRecords.builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, 0L);\n406:     }\n407: \n408:     /**\n409:      * Check if all batches in the queue are full.\n410:      */\n411:     private boolean allBatchesFull(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque) {\n412:         // Only the last batch may be incomplete, so we just check that.\n413:         ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\n414:         return last == null || last.isFull();\n415:     }\n416: \n417:      /**\n418:      *  Try to append to a ProducerBatch.\n419:      *\n420:      *  If it is full, we return null and a new batch is created. We also close the batch for record appends to free up\n421:      *  resources like compression buffers. The batch will be fully closed (ie. the record batch headers will be written\n422:      *  and memory records built) in one of the following cases (whichever comes first): right before send,\n423:      *  if it is expired, or when the producer is closed.\n424:      */\n425:     private RecordAppendResult tryAppend(long timestamp, byte[] key, byte[] value, Header[] headers,\n426:                                          Callback callback, Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, long nowMs) {\n427:         if (closed)\n428:             throw new KafkaException(\"Producer closed while send in progress\");\n429:         ProducerBatch last = deque.peekLast();\n430:         if (last != null) {\n431:             int initialBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes();\n432:             FutureRecordMetadata future = last.tryAppend(timestamp, key, value, headers, callback, nowMs);\n433:             if (future == null) {\n434:                 last.closeForRecordAppends();\n435:             } else {\n436:                 int appendedBytes = last.estimatedSizeInBytes() - initialBytes;\n437:                 return new RecordAppendResult(future, deque.size() > 1 || last.isFull(), false, appendedBytes);\n438:             }\n439:         }\n440:         return null;\n441:     }\n442: \n443:     private boolean isMuted(TopicPartition tp) {\n444:         return muted.contains(tp);\n445:     }\n446: \n447:     public void resetNextBatchExpiryTime() {\n448:         nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n449:     }\n450: \n451:     public void maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(ProducerBatch batch) {\n452:         if (batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs  > 0) {\n453:             // the non-negative check is to guard us against potential overflow due to setting\n454:             // a large value for deliveryTimeoutMs\n455:             nextBatchExpiryTimeMs = Math.min(nextBatchExpiryTimeMs, batch.createdMs + deliveryTimeoutMs);\n456:         } else {\n457:             log.warn(\"Skipping next batch expiry time update due to addition overflow: \"\n458:                 + \"batch.createMs={}, deliveryTimeoutMs={}\", batch.createdMs, deliveryTimeoutMs);\n459:         }\n460:     }\n461: \n462:     /**\n463:      * Get a list of batches which have been sitting in the accumulator too long and need to be expired.\n464:      */\n465:     public List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches(long now) {\n466:         List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = new ArrayList<>();\n467:         for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\n468:             for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\n469:                 // expire the batches in the order of sending\n470:                 synchronized (deque) {\n471:                     while (!deque.isEmpty()) {\n472:                         ProducerBatch batch = deque.getFirst();\n473:                         if (batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(deliveryTimeoutMs, now)) {\n474:                             deque.poll();\n475:                             batch.abortRecordAppends();\n476:                             expiredBatches.add(batch);\n477:                         } else {\n478:                             maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(batch);\n479:                             break;\n480:                         }\n481:                     }\n482:                 }\n483:             }\n484:         }\n485:         return expiredBatches;\n486:     }\n487: \n488:     public long getDeliveryTimeoutMs() {\n489:         return deliveryTimeoutMs;\n490:     }\n491: \n492:     /**\n493:      * Re-enqueue the given record batch in the accumulator. In Sender.completeBatch method, we check\n494:      * whether the batch has reached deliveryTimeoutMs or not. Hence we do not do the delivery timeout check here.\n495:      */\n496:     public void reenqueue(ProducerBatch batch, long now) {\n497:         batch.reenqueued(now);\n498:         Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getOrCreateDeque(batch.topicPartition);\n499:         synchronized (deque) {\n500:             if (transactionManager != null)\n501:                 insertInSequenceOrder(deque, batch);\n502:             else\n503:                 deque.addFirst(batch);\n504:         }\n505:     }\n506: \n507:     /**\n508:      * Split the big batch that has been rejected and reenqueue the split batches in to the accumulator.\n509:      * @return the number of split batches.\n510:      */\n511:     public int splitAndReenqueue(ProducerBatch bigBatch) {\n512:         // Reset the estimated compression ratio to the initial value or the big batch compression ratio, whichever\n513:         // is bigger. There are several different ways to do the reset. We chose the most conservative one to ensure\n514:         // the split doesn't happen too often.\n515:         CompressionRatioEstimator.setEstimation(bigBatch.topicPartition.topic(), compression.type(),\n516:                                                 Math.max(1.0f, (float) bigBatch.compressionRatio()));\n517:         Deque<ProducerBatch> dq = bigBatch.split(this.batchSize);\n518:         int numSplitBatches = dq.size();\n519:         Deque<ProducerBatch> partitionDequeue = getOrCreateDeque(bigBatch.topicPartition);\n520:         while (!dq.isEmpty()) {\n521:             ProducerBatch batch = dq.pollLast();\n522:             incomplete.add(batch);\n523:             // We treat the newly split batches as if they are not even tried.\n524:             synchronized (partitionDequeue) {\n525:                 if (transactionManager != null) {\n526:                     // We should track the newly created batches since they already have assigned sequences.\n527:                     transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\n528:                     insertInSequenceOrder(partitionDequeue, batch);\n529:                 } else {\n530:                     partitionDequeue.addFirst(batch);\n531:                 }\n532:             }\n533:         }\n534:         return numSplitBatches;\n535:     }\n536: \n537:     // We will have to do extra work to ensure the queue is in order when requests are being retried and there are\n538:     // multiple requests in flight to that partition. If the first in flight request fails to append, then all the\n539:     // subsequent in flight requests will also fail because the sequence numbers will not be accepted.\n540:     //\n541:     // Further, once batches are being retried, we are reduced to a single in flight request for that partition. So when\n542:     // the subsequent batches come back in sequence order, they will have to be placed further back in the queue.\n543:     //\n544:     // Note that this assumes that all the batches in the queue which have an assigned sequence also have the current\n545:     // producer id. We will not attempt to reorder messages if the producer id has changed, we will throw an\n546:     // IllegalStateException instead.\n547:     private void insertInSequenceOrder(Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, ProducerBatch batch) {\n548:         // When we are re-enqueueing and have enabled idempotence, the re-enqueued batch must always have a sequence.\n549:         if (batch.baseSequence() == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n550:             throw new IllegalStateException(\"Trying to re-enqueue a batch which doesn't have a sequence even \" +\n551:                 \"though idempotency is enabled.\");\n552: \n553:         if (!transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(batch.topicPartition))\n554:             throw new IllegalStateException(\"We are re-enqueueing a batch which is not tracked as part of the in flight \" +\n555:                 \"requests. batch.topicPartition: \" + batch.topicPartition + \"; batch.baseSequence: \" + batch.baseSequence());\n556: \n557:         ProducerBatch firstBatchInQueue = deque.peekFirst();\n558:         if (firstBatchInQueue != null && firstBatchInQueue.hasSequence() && firstBatchInQueue.baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence()) {\n559:             // The incoming batch can't be inserted at the front of the queue without violating the sequence ordering.\n560:             // This means that the incoming batch should be placed somewhere further back.\n561:             // We need to find the right place for the incoming batch and insert it there.\n562:             // We will only enter this branch if we have multiple inflights sent to different brokers and we need to retry\n563:             // the inflight batches.\n564:             //\n565:             // Since we reenqueue exactly one batch a time and ensure that the queue is ordered by sequence always, it\n566:             // is a simple linear scan of a subset of the in flight batches to find the right place in the queue each time.\n567:             List<ProducerBatch> orderedBatches = new ArrayList<>();\n568:             while (deque.peekFirst() != null && deque.peekFirst().hasSequence() && deque.peekFirst().baseSequence() < batch.baseSequence())\n569:                 orderedBatches.add(deque.pollFirst());\n570: \n571:             log.debug(\"Reordered incoming batch with sequence {} for partition {}. It was placed in the queue at \" +\n572:                 \"position {}\", batch.baseSequence(), batch.topicPartition, orderedBatches.size());\n573:             // Either we have reached a point where there are batches without a sequence (ie. never been drained\n574:             // and are hence in order by default), or the batch at the front of the queue has a sequence greater\n575:             // than the incoming batch. This is the right place to add the incoming batch.\n576:             deque.addFirst(batch);\n577: \n578:             // Now we have to re insert the previously queued batches in the right order.\n579:             for (int i = orderedBatches.size() - 1; i >= 0; --i) {\n580:                 deque.addFirst(orderedBatches.get(i));\n581:             }\n582: \n583:             // At this point, the incoming batch has been queued in the correct place according to its sequence.\n584:         } else {\n585:             deque.addFirst(batch);\n586:         }\n587:     }\n588: \n589:     /**\n590:      * Add the leader to the ready nodes if the batch is ready\n591:      *\n592:      * @param exhausted 'true' is the buffer pool is exhausted\n593:      * @param part The partition\n594:      * @param leader The leader for the partition\n595:      * @param waitedTimeMs How long batch waited\n596:      * @param backingOff Is backing off\n597:      * @param backoffAttempts Number of attempts for calculating backoff delay\n598:      * @param full Is batch full\n599:      * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\n600:      * @param readyNodes The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\n601:      * @return The delay for next check\n602:      */\n603:     private long batchReady(boolean exhausted, TopicPartition part, Node leader,\n604:                             long waitedTimeMs, boolean backingOff, int backoffAttempts,\n605:                             boolean full, long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes) {\n606:         if (!readyNodes.contains(leader) && !isMuted(part)) {\n607:             long timeToWaitMs = backingOff ? retryBackoff.backoff(backoffAttempts > 0 ? backoffAttempts - 1 : 0) : lingerMs;\n608:             boolean expired = waitedTimeMs >= timeToWaitMs;\n609:             boolean transactionCompleting = transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isCompleting();\n610:             boolean sendable = full\n611:                     || expired\n612:                     || exhausted\n613:                     || closed\n614:                     || flushInProgress()\n615:                     || transactionCompleting;\n616:             if (sendable && !backingOff) {\n617:                 readyNodes.add(leader);\n618:             } else {\n619:                 long timeLeftMs = Math.max(timeToWaitMs - waitedTimeMs, 0);\n620:                 // Note that this results in a conservative estimate since an un-sendable partition may have\n621:                 // a leader that will later be found to have sendable data. However, this is good enough\n622:                 // since we'll just wake up and then sleep again for the remaining time.\n623:                 nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Math.min(timeLeftMs, nextReadyCheckDelayMs);\n624:             }\n625:         }\n626:         return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\n627:     }\n628: \n629:     /**\n630:      * Iterate over partitions to see which one have batches ready and collect leaders of those\n631:      * partitions into the set of ready nodes.  If partition has no leader, add the topic to the set\n632:      * of topics with no leader.  This function also calculates stats for adaptive partitioning.\n633:      *\n634:      * @param metadataSnapshot      The cluster metadata\n635:      * @param nowMs                 The current time\n636:      * @param topic                 The topic\n637:      * @param topicInfo             The topic info\n638:      * @param nextReadyCheckDelayMs The delay for next check\n639:      * @param readyNodes            The set of ready nodes (to be filled in)\n640:      * @param unknownLeaderTopics   The set of topics with no leader (to be filled in)\n641:      * @return The delay for next check\n642:      */\n643:     private long partitionReady(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, long nowMs, String topic,\n644:                                 TopicInfo topicInfo,\n645:                                 long nextReadyCheckDelayMs, Set<Node> readyNodes, Set<String> unknownLeaderTopics) {\n646:         ConcurrentMap<Integer, Deque<ProducerBatch>> batches = topicInfo.batches;\n647:         // Collect the queue sizes for available partitions to be used in adaptive partitioning.\n648:         int[] queueSizes = null;\n649:         int[] partitionIds = null;\n650:         if (enableAdaptivePartitioning && batches.size() >= metadataSnapshot.cluster().partitionsForTopic(topic).size()) {\n651:             // We don't do adaptive partitioning until we scheduled at least a batch for all\n652:             // partitions (i.e. we have the corresponding entries in the batches map), we just\n653:             // do uniform.  The reason is that we build queue sizes from the batches map,\n654:             // and if an entry is missing in the batches map, then adaptive partitioning logic\n655:             // won't know about it and won't switch to it.\n656:             queueSizes = new int[batches.size()];\n657:             partitionIds = new int[queueSizes.length];\n658:         }\n659: \n660:         int queueSizesIndex = -1;\n661:         boolean exhausted = this.free.queued() > 0;\n662:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, Deque<ProducerBatch>> entry : batches.entrySet()) {\n663:             TopicPartition part = new TopicPartition(topic, entry.getKey());\n664:             // Advance queueSizesIndex so that we properly index available\n665:             // partitions.  Do it here so that it's done for all code paths.\n666: \n667:             Node leader = metadataSnapshot.cluster().leaderFor(part);\n668:             if (leader != null && queueSizes != null) {\n669:                 ++queueSizesIndex;\n670:                 assert queueSizesIndex < queueSizes.length;\n671:                 partitionIds[queueSizesIndex] = part.partition();\n672:             }\n673: \n674:             Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = entry.getValue();\n675: \n676:             final long waitedTimeMs;\n677:             final boolean backingOff;\n678:             final int backoffAttempts;\n679:             final int dequeSize;\n680:             final boolean full;\n681: \n682:             OptionalInt leaderEpoch = metadataSnapshot.leaderEpochFor(part);\n683: \n684:             // This loop is especially hot with large partition counts. So -\n685: \n686:             // 1. We should avoid code that increases synchronization between application thread calling\n687:             // send(), and background thread running runOnce(), see https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-16226\n688: \n689:             // 2. We are careful to only perform the minimum required inside the\n690:             // synchronized block, as this lock is also used to synchronize producer threads\n691:             // attempting to append() to a partition/batch.\n692: \n693:             synchronized (deque) {\n694:                 // Deques are often empty in this path, esp with large partition counts,\n695:                 // so we exit early if we can.\n696:                 ProducerBatch batch = deque.peekFirst();\n697:                 if (batch == null) {\n698:                     continue;\n699:                 }\n700: \n701:                 waitedTimeMs = batch.waitedTimeMs(nowMs);\n702:                 batch.maybeUpdateLeaderEpoch(leaderEpoch);\n703:                 backingOff = shouldBackoff(batch.hasLeaderChangedForTheOngoingRetry(), batch, waitedTimeMs);\n704:                 backoffAttempts = batch.attempts();\n705:                 dequeSize = deque.size();\n706:                 full = dequeSize > 1 || batch.isFull();\n707:             }\n708: \n709:             if (leader == null) {\n710:                 // This is a partition for which leader is not known, but messages are available to send.\n711:                 // Note that entries are currently not removed from batches when deque is empty.\n712:                 unknownLeaderTopics.add(part.topic());\n713:             } else {\n714:                 if (queueSizes != null)\n715:                     queueSizes[queueSizesIndex] = dequeSize;\n716:                 if (partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs > 0) {\n717:                     // Check if we want to exclude the partition from the list of available partitions\n718:                     // if the broker hasn't responded for some time.\n719:                     NodeLatencyStats nodeLatencyStats = nodeStats.get(leader.id());\n720:                     if (nodeLatencyStats != null) {\n721:                         // NOTE: there is no synchronization between reading metrics,\n722:                         // so we read ready time first to avoid accidentally marking partition\n723:                         // unavailable if we read while the metrics are being updated.\n724:                         long readyTimeMs = nodeLatencyStats.readyTimeMs;\n725:                         if (readyTimeMs - nodeLatencyStats.drainTimeMs > partitionAvailabilityTimeoutMs)\n726:                             --queueSizesIndex;\n727:                     }\n728:                 }\n729: \n730:                 nextReadyCheckDelayMs = batchReady(exhausted, part, leader, waitedTimeMs, backingOff,\n731:                     backoffAttempts, full, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes);\n732:             }\n733:         }\n734: \n735:         // We've collected the queue sizes for partitions of this topic, now we can calculate\n736:         // load stats.  NOTE: the stats are calculated in place, modifying the\n737:         // queueSizes array.\n738:         topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionLoadStats(queueSizes, partitionIds, queueSizesIndex + 1);\n739:         return nextReadyCheckDelayMs;\n740:     }\n741: \n742:     /**\n743:      * Get a list of nodes whose partitions are ready to be sent, and the earliest time at which any non-sendable\n744:      * partition will be ready; Also return the flag for whether there are any unknown leaders for the accumulated\n745:      * partition batches.\n746:      * <p>\n747:      * A destination node is ready to send data if:\n748:      * <ol>\n749:      * <li>There is at least one partition that is not backing off its send\n750:      * <li><b>and</b> those partitions are not muted (to prevent reordering if\n751:      *   {@value org.apache.kafka.clients.producer.ProducerConfig#MAX_IN_FLIGHT_REQUESTS_PER_CONNECTION}\n752:      *   is set to one)</li>\n753:      * <li><b>and <i>any</i></b> of the following are true</li>\n754:      * <ul>\n755:      *     <li>The record set is full</li>\n756:      *     <li>The record set has sat in the accumulator for at least lingerMs milliseconds</li>\n757:      *     <li>The accumulator is out of memory and threads are blocking waiting for data (in this case all partitions\n758:      *     are immediately considered ready).</li>\n759:      *     <li>The accumulator has been closed</li>\n760:      * </ul>\n761:      * </ol>\n762:      */\n763:     public ReadyCheckResult ready(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, long nowMs) {\n764:         Set<Node> readyNodes = new HashSet<>();\n765:         long nextReadyCheckDelayMs = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n766:         Set<String> unknownLeaderTopics = new HashSet<>();\n767:         // Go topic by topic so that we can get queue sizes for partitions in a topic and calculate\n768:         // cumulative frequency table (used in partitioner).\n769:         for (Map.Entry<String, TopicInfo> topicInfoEntry : this.topicInfoMap.entrySet()) {\n770:             final String topic = topicInfoEntry.getKey();\n771:             nextReadyCheckDelayMs = partitionReady(metadataSnapshot, nowMs, topic, topicInfoEntry.getValue(), nextReadyCheckDelayMs, readyNodes, unknownLeaderTopics);\n772:         }\n773:         return new ReadyCheckResult(readyNodes, nextReadyCheckDelayMs, unknownLeaderTopics);\n774:     }\n775: \n776:     /**\n777:      * Check whether there are any batches which haven't been drained\n778:      */\n779:     public boolean hasUndrained() {\n780:         for (TopicInfo topicInfo : topicInfoMap.values()) {\n781:             for (Deque<ProducerBatch> deque : topicInfo.batches.values()) {\n782:                 synchronized (deque) {\n783:                     if (!deque.isEmpty())\n784:                         return true;\n785:                 }\n786:             }\n787:         }\n788:         return false;\n789:     }\n790: \n791:     private boolean shouldBackoff(boolean hasLeaderChanged, final ProducerBatch batch, final long waitedTimeMs) {\n792:         boolean shouldWaitMore = batch.attempts() > 0 && waitedTimeMs < retryBackoff.backoff(batch.attempts() - 1);\n793:         boolean shouldBackoff = !hasLeaderChanged && shouldWaitMore;\n794:         if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\n795:             if (shouldBackoff) {\n796:                 log.trace(\n797:                     \"For {}, will backoff\", batch);\n798:             } else {\n799:                 log.trace(\n800:                     \"For {}, will not backoff, shouldWaitMore {}, hasLeaderChanged {}\", batch,\n801:                     shouldWaitMore, hasLeaderChanged);\n802:             }\n803:         } else if (log.isDebugEnabled() && hasLeaderChanged) {\n804:             // Add less-verbose log at DEBUG.\n805:             log.debug(\"For {}, leader has changed, hence skipping backoff.\", batch);\n806:         }\n807:         return shouldBackoff;\n808:     }\n809: \n810:     private boolean shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition(ProducerBatch first, TopicPartition tp) {\n811:         ProducerIdAndEpoch producerIdAndEpoch;\n812:         if (transactionManager != null) {\n813:             if (!transactionManager.isSendToPartitionAllowed(tp))\n814:                 return true;\n815: \n816:             producerIdAndEpoch = transactionManager.producerIdAndEpoch();\n817:             if (!producerIdAndEpoch.isValid())\n818:                 // we cannot send the batch until we have refreshed the producer id\n819:                 return true;\n820: \n821:             if (!first.hasSequence()) {\n822:                 if (transactionManager.hasInflightBatches(tp) && transactionManager.hasStaleProducerIdAndEpoch(tp)) {\n823:                     // Don't drain any new batches while the partition has in-flight batches with a different epoch\n824:                     // and/or producer ID. Otherwise, a batch with a new epoch and sequence number\n825:                     // 0 could be written before earlier batches complete, which would cause out of sequence errors\n826:                     return true;\n827:                 }\n828: \n829:                 if (transactionManager.hasUnresolvedSequence(first.topicPartition))\n830:                     // Don't drain any new batches while the state of previous sequence numbers\n831:                     // is unknown. The previous batches would be unknown if they were aborted\n832:                     // on the client after being sent to the broker at least once.\n833:                     return true;\n834:             }\n835: \n836:             int firstInFlightSequence = transactionManager.firstInFlightSequence(first.topicPartition);\n837:             // If the queued batch already has an assigned sequence, then it is being retried.\n838:             // In this case, we wait until the next immediate batch is ready and drain that.\n839:             // We only move on when the next in line batch is complete (either successfully or due to\n840:             // a fatal broker error). This effectively reduces our in flight request count to 1.\n841:             return firstInFlightSequence != RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE && first.hasSequence()\n842:                     && first.baseSequence() != firstInFlightSequence;\n843:         }\n844:         return false;\n845:     }\n846: \n847:     private List<ProducerBatch> drainBatchesForOneNode(MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot, Node node, int maxSize, long now) {\n848:         int size = 0;\n849:         List<PartitionInfo> parts = metadataSnapshot.cluster().partitionsForNode(node.id());\n850:         List<ProducerBatch> ready = new ArrayList<>();\n851:         if (parts.isEmpty())\n852:             return ready;\n853:         /* to make starvation less likely each node has it's own drainIndex */\n854:         int drainIndex = getDrainIndex(node.idString());\n855:         int start = drainIndex = drainIndex % parts.size();\n856:         do {\n857:             PartitionInfo part = parts.get(drainIndex);\n858: \n859:             TopicPartition tp = new TopicPartition(part.topic(), part.partition());\n860:             updateDrainIndex(node.idString(), drainIndex);\n861:             drainIndex = (drainIndex + 1) % parts.size();\n862:             // Only proceed if the partition has no in-flight batches.\n863:             if (isMuted(tp))\n864:                 continue;\n865:             Deque<ProducerBatch> deque = getDeque(tp);\n866:             if (deque == null)\n867:                 continue;\n868: \n869:             OptionalInt leaderEpoch = metadataSnapshot.leaderEpochFor(tp);\n870: \n871:             final ProducerBatch batch;\n872:             synchronized (deque) {\n873:                 // invariant: !isMuted(tp,now) && deque != null\n874:                 ProducerBatch first = deque.peekFirst();\n875:                 if (first == null)\n876:                     continue;\n877: \n878:                 // first != null\n879:                 // Only drain the batch if it is not during backoff period.\n880:                 first.maybeUpdateLeaderEpoch(leaderEpoch);\n881:                 if (shouldBackoff(first.hasLeaderChangedForTheOngoingRetry(), first, first.waitedTimeMs(now)))\n882:                     continue;\n883: \n884:                 if (size + first.estimatedSizeInBytes() > maxSize && !ready.isEmpty()) {\n885:                     // there is a rare case that a single batch size is larger than the request size due to\n886:                     // compression; in this case we will still eventually send this batch in a single request\n887:                     break;\n888:                 } else {\n889:                     if (shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition(first, tp))\n890:                         break;\n891:                 }\n892: \n893:                 batch = deque.pollFirst();\n894: \n895:                 boolean isTransactional = transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional();\n896:                 ProducerIdAndEpoch producerIdAndEpoch =\n897:                     transactionManager != null ? transactionManager.producerIdAndEpoch() : null;\n898:                 if (producerIdAndEpoch != null && !batch.hasSequence()) {\n899:                     // If the producer id/epoch of the partition do not match the latest one\n900:                     // of the producer, we update it and reset the sequence. This should be\n901:                     // only done when all its in-flight batches have completed. This is guarantee\n902:                     // in `shouldStopDrainBatchesForPartition`.\n903:                     transactionManager.maybeUpdateProducerIdAndEpoch(batch.topicPartition);\n904: \n905:                     // If the batch already has an assigned sequence, then we should not change the producer id and\n906:                     // sequence number, since this may introduce duplicates. In particular, the previous attempt\n907:                     // may actually have been accepted, and if we change the producer id and sequence here, this\n908:                     // attempt will also be accepted, causing a duplicate.\n909:                     //\n910:                     // Additionally, we update the next sequence number bound for the partition, and also have\n911:                     // the transaction manager track the batch so as to ensure that sequence ordering is maintained\n912:                     // even if we receive out of order responses.\n913:                     batch.setProducerState(producerIdAndEpoch, transactionManager.sequenceNumber(batch.topicPartition), isTransactional);\n914:                     transactionManager.incrementSequenceNumber(batch.topicPartition, batch.recordCount);\n915:                     log.debug(\"Assigned producerId {} and producerEpoch {} to batch with base sequence \" +\n916:                             \"{} being sent to partition {}\", producerIdAndEpoch.producerId,\n917:                         producerIdAndEpoch.epoch, batch.baseSequence(), tp);\n918: \n919:                     transactionManager.addInFlightBatch(batch);\n920:                 }\n921:             }\n922: \n923:             // the rest of the work by processing outside the lock\n924:             // close() is particularly expensive\n925:             batch.close();\n926:             size += batch.records().sizeInBytes();\n927:             ready.add(batch);\n928: \n929: retried, it will be retried to a newer leader.\\n128:      */\\n129: \\n130:     boolean hasLeaderChangedForTheOngoingRetry() {\\n131:         int attempts = attempts();\\n132:         boolean isRetry = attempts >= 1;\\n133:         if (!isRetry)\\n134:             return false;\\n135:         return attempts == attemptsWhenLeaderLastChanged;\\n136:     }\\n137: \\n138: \\n139:     /**\\n140: isn't sufficient room.\\n143:      */\\n144:     public FutureRecordMetadata tryAppend(long timestamp, byte[] key, byte[] value, Header[] headers, Callback callback, long now) {\\n145:         if (!recordsBuilder.hasRoomFor(timestamp, key, value, headers)) {\\n146:             return null;\\n147:         } else {\\n148:             this.recordsBuilder.append(timestamp, key, value,                                                       timestamp,\\n154:                                                                    key == null ? -1 : key.length,\\n155:                                                                    value == null ? -1 : value.length,\\n156:                                                                    Time.SYSTEM);\\n157:             // we have to keep every future returned to the users in case the batch needs to be\\n158:             // split to several new batches and resent.\\n159:             thunks.add(new Thunk(callback, future));\\n160:             this.recordCount++;\\n161:             return future;\\n162:         }\\n163:     }\\n164: \\n165:     /**\\n166:      * This method is only used by {@link #split(int)} when splitting a large batch to smaller ones.\\n167:      * @return true if the record has been successfully appended, false otherwise.\\n168:      */\\n169:     private boolean tryAppendForSplit(long timestamp, ByteBuffer key, ByteBuffer value, Header[] headers, Thunk thunk) {\\n170:         if (!recordsBuilder.hasRoomFor(timestamp, key, value, headers)) {\\n171:             return false;\\n172:         } else {\\n173:             // No need to get the CRC.\\n174:             this.recordsBuilder.append(timestamp, key, value, headers);\\n175:             this.maxRecordSize = Math.max(this.maxRecordSize, AbstractRecords.estimateSizeInBytesUpperBound(magic(),\\n176:                     recordsBuilder.compression().type(), key, value, headers));\\n177:             FutureRecordMetadata future = new finalState.get());\\n198: \\n199:         log.trace(\\\"Aborting batch for partition {}\\\", topicPartition, exception);\\n200:         completeFutureAndFireCallbacks(ProduceResponse.INVALID_OFFSET, Final state, once set, is immutable. This function may be called\\n242:      * once or twice on a batch. It may be called twice if\\n243:      * 1. An inflight batch expires before a response from the broker is received. The batch's final\\n244:      * state is set to FAILED. But it could succeed on the broker and second time around batch.done() may\\n245:      * try to set SUCCEEDED final state.\\n246:      * 2. If a transaction abortion happens or if the producer is closed forcefully, the final state is\\n247:      * ABORTED but again it could succeed if broker responds with a success.\\n248:      *\\n249:      * Attempted transitions from [FAILED | ABORTED] --> SUCCEEDED are logged.\\n250:      * Attempted transitions from one failure state to the same or a different failed state are ignored.\\n251:      * Attempted transitions from SUCCEEDED to the same or a failed state throw an exception.\\n252:      *\\n253:      * @param baseOffset The base offset of the messages assigned by the server\\n254:      * @param logAppendTime The log append time or -1 if CreateTime is being used\\n255:      * @param topLevelException The exception that occurred (or null if the request was successful)\\n256:      * @param recordExceptions Record exception function mapping batchIndex to the respective record exception\\n257:      * @return true if the batch was completed successfully and false if the batch was previously aborted\\n258:      */\\n259:     private boolean done(\\n260:         long baseOffset,\\n261:         long logAppendTime,\\n262:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n263:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions\\n264:     ) {\\n265:         final FinalState tryFinalState = (topLevelException == null) ? FinalState.SUCCEEDED : FinalState.FAILED;\\n266:         if (tryFinalState == FinalState.SUCCEEDED) {\\n267:             log.trace(\\\"Successfully produced messages to {} with base offset {}.\\\",        }\\n271: \\n272:         if (this.finalState.compareAndSet(null, tryFinalState)) {\\n273:             completeFutureAndFireCallbacks(baseOffset, logAppendTime, recordExceptions);\\n274: }\\n356: \\n357:     private long sendProducerData(long now) {\\n358:         MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\\n359:         // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\\n360:         RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\\n361: \\n362:         // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\\n363:         if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\\n364:             // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as to send to\\n376:         Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\\n377:         long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\\n378:         while (iter.hasNext()) {\\n379:             Node node \\n565:     /**\\n566:      * Handle a produce response\\n567:      */\\n568:     private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\\n569:         RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\\n570:         int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\\n571:         if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\\n572:             log.trace(\\\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\\\",\\n573:                 requestHeader, {\\n584:             log.warn(\\\"Cancelled request {} due to a version mismatch with node {}\\\",\\n585:                     response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\\n586:             for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\\n587:                 completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\\n588:         } else {\\n589:             log.trace(\\\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\\\", response.destination(), correlationId);\\n590:             // if we have a response, parse it\\n591:             if (response.hasResponse()) {\\n592:                 // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\\n593:                 // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\\n594:                 ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\\n595:                 // This will be set by completeBatch.\\n596:                 Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\\n597:                 produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\\n598:                     ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\\n599:                             Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\\n600:                             p.baseOffset(),\\n601:                             p.logAppendTimeMs(),\\n602:                             p.logStartOffset(),\\n603:                             p.recordErrors()\\n604:                                 .stream()\\n605:                                 .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\\n606:                                 .collect(Collectors.toList()),\\n607:                             p.errorMessage(),\\n608:                             p.currentLeader());\\n609: \\n610:                     // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\\n611:                     // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\\n612:                     // topic name in the response will be empty.\\n613:                     // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\\n614:                     TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\\n615:                             new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\\n616:                             new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\\n617: \\n618:                     ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\\n619:                     if (batch == null) {\\n620:                         throw new IllegalStateException(\\\"Can't find batch created for topic id \\\" + r.topicId() +\\n621:                                 \\\" topic name \\\" + r.name() + \\\" partition \\\" + p.index() + \\\" using \\\" + topicNames);\\n622:                     }\\n623:                     completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\\n624:                 }));\\n625: \\n626:                 if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\\n627:                     List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\\n628:                         .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\\n629:                         .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\\n630:                         .collect(\\n631:                             Collectors.toList());\\n632:                     Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\\n633:                     if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n634:                         updatedPartitions.forEach(\\n635:                             part -> log.debug(\\\"For {} leader was updated.\\\", part)\\n636:                         );\\n637:                     }\\n638:                 }\\n639: \\n640:                 this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\\n641:             } else {\\n642:                 // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\\n643:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\\n644:                     completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\\n645:                 }\\n646:             }\\n647:         }\\n648:     }\\n649: \\n650:     /**\\n651:      * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\\n652:      *\\n653:      * @param batch The record batch\\n654:      * @param response The produce response\\n655:      * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\\n656:      * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\\n657:      * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\\n658:      */\\n659:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\\n660:                                long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\\n661:         Errors error = response.error;\\n662: \\n663:         if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\\n664:                 (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\\n665:             // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\\n666:             // the retry attempts in this case.\\n667:             log.warn(\\n668:                 \\\"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n669:                 correlationId,\\n670:                 batch.topicPartition,\\n671:                 this.retries - batch.attempts(),\\n672:                 formatErrMsg(response));\\n673:             if (transactionManager != null)\\n674:                 transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\\n675:             this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\\n676:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n677:             this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\\n678:         } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\\n679:             if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\\n680:                 log.warn(\\n681:                     \\\"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\\\",\\n682:                     correlationId,\\n683:                     batch.topicPartition,\\n684:                     this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\\n685:                     formatErrMsg(response));\\n686:                 reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\\n687:             } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\\n688:                 // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\\n689:                 // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\\n690:                 // the correct offset and timestamp.\\n691:                 //\\n692:                 // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\\n693:                 completeBatch(batch, response);\\n694:             } else {\\n695:                 // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\\n696:                 // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\\n697:                 // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\\n698:                 failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\\n699:             }\\n700:             if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\\n701:                 if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\\n702:                     log.warn(\\\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \\\" +\\n703:                             \\\"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\\\",\\n704:                         batch.topicPartition);\\n705:                 } else {\\n706:                     log.warn(\\\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \\\" +\\n707:                             \\\"to request metadata update now\\\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\\n708:                 }\\n709:                 if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\\n710:                     log.debug(\\\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\\\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\\n711:                     if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\\n712:                         && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\\n713:                         partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\\n714:                             Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\\n715:                     }\\n716:                 }\\n717:                 metadata.requestUpdate(false);\\n718:             }\\n719:         } else {\\n720:             completeBatch(batch, response);\\n721:         }\\n722: \\n723:         // Unmute the completed partition.\\n724:         if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\\n725:             this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\\n726:     }\\n727: \\n728:     /**\\n729:      * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\\n730:      * e.g \\\"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\\\"\\n731:      */\\n732:     private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n733:         String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\\n734:                 \\\"\\\" : String.format(\\\". Error Message: %s\\\", response.errorMessage);\\n735:         return String.format(\\\"%s%s\\\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\\n736:     }\\n737: \\n738:     private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\\n739:         this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\\n740:         maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\\n741:         this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n742:     }\\n743: \\n744:     private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\\n745:         if (transactionManager != null) {\\n746:             transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\\n747:         }\\n748: \\n749:         if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\\n750:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n751:         }\\n752:     }\\n753: \\n754:     private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\\n755:                            ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\\n756:                            boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\\n757:         final RuntimeException topLevelException;\\n758:         if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n759:             topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\\n760:         else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\\n761:             topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\\\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\\\");\\n762:         else\\n763:             topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\\n764: \\n765:         if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\\n766:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n767:         } else {\\n768:             Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\\n769:             for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\\n770:                 // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\\n771:                 // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\\n772:                 // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\\n773:                 // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\\n774:                 final String errorMessage;\\n775:                 if (recordError.message != null) {\\n776:                     errorMessage = recordError.message;\\n777:                 } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\\n778:                     errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\\n779:                 } else {\\n780:                     errorMessage = response.error.message();\\n781:                 }\\n782: \\n783:                 // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\\n784:                 // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\\n785:                 if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\\n786:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\\n787:                 } else {\\n788:                     recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\\n789:                 }\\n790:             }\\n791: \\n792:             Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\\n793:                 RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\\n794:                 if (exception != null) {\\n795:                     return exception;\\n796:                 } else {\\n797:                     // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\\n798:                     // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\\n799:                     // return a generic exception.\\n800:                     return new KafkaException(\\\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \\\" +\\n801:                         \\\"which had one more more invalid records\\\");\\n802:                 }\\n803:             };\\n804: \\n805:             failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n806:         }\\n807:     }\\n808: \\n809:     private void failBatch(\\n810:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n811:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n812:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n813:     ) {\\n814:         failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n815:     }\\n816: \\n817:     private void failBatch(\\n818:         ProducerBatch batch,\\n819:         RuntimeException topLevelException,\\n820:         Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\\n821:         boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\\n822:     ) {\\n823:         this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\\n824: \\n825:         if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\\n826:             if (transactionManager != null) {\\n827:                 try {\\n828:                     // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\\n829:                     // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\\n830:                     transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\\n831:                 } catch (Exception e) {\\n832:                     log.debug(\\\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\\\", e);\\n833:                 }\\n834:             }\\n835:             maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\\n836:         }\\n837:     }\\n838: \\n839:     /**\\n840:      * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\\n841:      * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\\n842:      * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\\n843:      */\\n844:     private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\\n845:         return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\\n846:             batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\\n847:             !batch.isDone() &&\\n848:             (transactionManager == null ?\\n849:                     response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\\n850:                     transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\\n851:     }\\n852: \\n853:     /**\\n854:      * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\\n855:      */\\n856:     private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\\n857:         for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\\n858:             sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\\n859:     }\\n860: \\n861:     /**\\n862:      * Create a produce request from the given record batches\\n863:      */\\n864:     private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n865:         if (batches.isEmpty())\\n866:             return;\\n867: \\n868:         final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\\n869:         Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\\n870: \\n871:         ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\\n872:         for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\\n873:             TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\\n874:             MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\\n875:             Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\\n876:             ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData tpData = tpd.find(tp.topic(), topicId);\\n877: \\n878:             if (tpData == null) {\\n879:                 tpData = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData()\\n880:                         .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\\n881:                 tpd.add(tpData);\\n882:             }\\n883: \\n884:             tpData.partitionData().add(new ProduceRequestData.PartitionProduceData()\\n885:                     .setIndex(tp.partition())\\n886:                     .setRecords(records));\\n887:             recordsByPartition.put(tp, batch);\\n888:         }\\n889: \\n890:         String transactionalId = null;\\n891:         boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\\n892:         if (transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional()) {\\n893:             transactionalId = transactionManager.transactionalId();\\n894:             useTransactionV1Version = !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\\n895:         }\\n896: \\n897:         ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\\n898:                 new ProduceRequestData()\\n899:                         .setAcks(acks)\\n900:                         .setTimeoutMs(timeout)\\n901:                         .setTransactionalId(transactionalId)\\n902:                         .setTopicData(tpd),\\n903:                 useTransactionV1Version\\n904:         );\\n905:         // Fetch topic names from metadata outside callback as topic ids may change during the callback\\n906:         // for example if topic was recreated.\\n907:         Map<Uuid, String> topicNames = metadata.topicNames();\\n908: \\n909:         RequestCompletionHandler callback = response -> handleProduceResponse(response, recordsByPartition, topicNames, time.milliseconds());\\n910: \\n911:         String nodeId = Integer.toString(destination);\\n912:         ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(nodeId, requestBuilder, now, acks != 0,\\n913:                 requestTimeoutMs, callback);\\n914:         client.send(clientRequest, now);\\n915:         log.trace(\\\"Sent produce request to {}: {}\\\", nodeId, requestBuilder);\\n916:     }\\n917: \\n918:     private Map<String, Uuid> topicIdsForBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\\n919:         return batches.stream()\\n920:                 .collect(Collectors.toMap(\\n921:                         b -> b.topicPartition.topic(),\\n922:                         b -> metadata.topicIds().getOrDefault(b.topicPartition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID),\\n923:                         (existing, replacement) -> replacement)\\n924:                 );\\n925:     }\\n926: \\n927:     /**\\n928:      * Wake up the selector associated with this send thread\\n929:      */\\n930:     public void wakeup() {\\n931:         this.client.wakeup();\\n932:     }\\n933: \\n934:     public   public void updateProduceRequestMetrics(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches) {\\n1037:             long now = time.milliseconds();\\n1038:             for (List<ProducerBatch> nodeBatch : batches.values()) {\\n1039:                 int records = 0;\\n1040:                 for (ProducerBatch batch : nodeBatch) {\\n1041:                     // register all per-topic metrics at        log.debug(\"Starting Kafka producer I/O thread.\");\n238: \n239:         // main loop, runs until close is called\n240:         while (running) {\n241:             try {\n242:                 runOnce();\n243:             } catch (Exception e) {\n244:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n245:             }\n246:         }\n247: \n248: in the transaction manager, accumulator or waiting for acknowledgment,\n252:         // wait until these are completed.\n253:         while (!forceClose && ((this.accumulator.hasUndrained() || this.client.inFlightRequestCount() > 0) || hasPendingTransactionalRequests())) {\n254:             try {\n255:                 runOnce();\n256:             } catch (Exception e) {\n257: {\n264:                 log.info(\"Aborting incomplete transaction due to shutdown\");\n265:                 try {\n266:                     // It is possible for the transaction manager to throw errors when aborting. Catch these\n267:                     // so as not to interfere with the rest of the shutdown logic.\n268:                     transactionManager.beginAbort();\n269:                 } catch (Exception e) {\n270:                     log.error(\"Error in kafka producer I/O thread while aborting transaction when during closing: \", e);\n271:                     // Force close in case the transactionManager is in error states.\n272:                     forceClose = true;\n273:                 }\n274:             }\n275:             try {\n276:                 runOnce();\n277:             } catch (Exception e) {\n278:                 log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n279:             }\n280:         }\n281: \n282:         if (forceClose) {\n283: {\n286:                 log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete transactional requests due to forced shutdown\");\n287:                 transactionManager.close();\n288:             }\n289:
